###Issue of Melwys### II
150159 = {
	name = "Прентис"	#Canon
	dynasty = 159

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "riverlander"

	father = 16159
	mother = 46159

	add_trait = underhanded_rogue
	add_trait = proud
	add_trait = ambitious

	8020.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	8036.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = poor_warrior }
	8043.1.1 = { #Faith Militant Uprising
		add_spouse = 450159
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8043.5.10 } }
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_vassal = { set_character_flag = supporting_king }
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8048.3.1 = { #Rogar Baratheon Rebellion
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8048.3.7 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				any_vassal = {
					set_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = against_king
				}
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
		}
	}
	8059.2.1 = {
		add_trait = "ill"
		death = { death_reason = death_trait } # Died of Shivers
	}
}

###Issue of Edmyn### III
15159 = {
	name = "Гровер"	# Grandfather of Elmo. Great Grandfather of Kermit, lord During the Dance
	dynasty = 159

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "riverlander"

	father = 150159
	mother = 450159

	add_trait = tough_soldier
	add_trait = wroth
	add_trait = stubborn

	8049.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			health = 4
		}
	}
	8065.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = poor_warrior }
	8068.1.1 = { add_spouse = 60800149 } #Bracken, as another possible reason why he supported greens
	8110.1.1 = { add_trait = blinded_age }
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		add_trait = incapable
		effect = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { character = 14159 }
				give_minor_title = title_regent
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.5.5 } }
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
				set_defacto_liege = THIS
				any_vassal = {
					set_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = against_king
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_dithered
							who = ROOT
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.5.5 = {
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = {
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_dithered
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			any_vassal = {
				clr_character_flag = neutral
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.6.5 = { death = yes }
}

###Issue of Elmo### VI
13159 = {
	name = "Кермит"	# Medgar grandfather. Lord of Riverrun at the time of the Dornish Conquest.
	dynasty = 159

	martial = 7

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "riverlander"

	add_trait = "quick_1"
	add_trait = "brave"
	add_trait = "diligent"
	add_trait = "authoritative"
	add_trait = "proud"
	add_trait = "skilled_tactician"

	father = 14159 # Elmo Tully
	mother = 44159

	8112.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	8128.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = skilled_warrior } #Killed Borros Baratheon
	8130.7.14 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		create_bloodline = {
			type = kermit_tully
			has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		}
		effect = { set_character_flag = kermit_tully }
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}

			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
			}
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {
		death = { # Killed in the Dance of Dragons.
			death_reason = death_duel
			killer = 350225 #Adrian Tarbeck
		}
	}
}

25178457 = {
	name = "Брайан"	# a lord, at the time of Dance of Dragons. He sided with Rhaenyra
	dynasty = 178457

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "riverlander"

	father = 24178457

	8093.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	8109.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = trained_warrior }
	8118.1.1 = { add_spouse = 114178452 }	#Morya Bigglestone
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.5.5 } } #Lord Tully joined war on the same side
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8134.1.1 = { death = yes }
}
